    Code
      tbl %>% add_stat_label(location = "column", label = all_categorical() ~
        "no. (%)") %>% render_as_html()

    Code
      tbl %>% add_overall() %>% add_stat_label() %>% render_as_html()

    Code
      tbl %>% add_stat_label(location = "column", label = all_categorical() ~
        "no. (%)") %>% render_as_html()

        "no. (%)") %>% render_as_html()

    Code
      tbl %>% add_stat_label(location = "column", label = all_categorical() ~
        "no. (%)") %>% render_as_html()

      tbl1 %>% render_as_html()
